POGUE, Robert Adner, (26 Mar) 1906 - 11 Jun 1982. (Maury Co. Hampshire, native; s/o Allie Pogue (1874 - 1936) & Susan Angeline "Angie" Brooks Pogue (1878 - 1949); h/o Lura W. Whiteside Pogue (1908 - 2005), mar. 6 May 1939; In 1928 the Isom School with South Point School formed the new Stephens School. There were four teacher at Stephens School, Robert Pogue taught grades seven and eight and coached the basketball team. The basketball court was a dirt court on the left side of the Stephens school between the school and the road was the baseball diamond; Robert was also the bus driver, the children called the bus "Old White Top" and was an old flat bed truck that someone had converted into a bus. Seats had been installed and it had tarpaulin sides that could be rolled up in the summertime. In 1942 Robert accepted a job as principal of Mynders School just south of Columbia, his wife Lura taught there as well, at first they lived in an apartment in the school and later bought a house in Columbia; Robert was drafted into the U. Most listings in this  (the currently most active cemetery in Maury County) cemetery are updates from Mary Bob McClain of Birmingham, AL from various sources such as Obituaries & Funeral Home Records, and do not necessarily detail the tombstone inscriptions. These listings are continually being updated and are subject to change at any time. We strive for accuracy and accept corrections. If you see anything wrong here tell us so we will fix it.
